NOTIFICATIONS  BY  GOVERNMENT
ANIMAL HUSBANDRY, DAIRYING AND FISHERIES
DEPARTMENT.
Notification regarding four members elected among
themselves by Veterinary Practitioners Registered in
the State Veterinary Registers as members to the
Tamil Nadu Veterinary Council under Indian Veterinary
Council Act.
[G.O. Ms. No. 132, Animal Husbandry, Dairying and
Fisheries (AH3-2), 4th November 2009.]
No. II(2)/AHDFI/609/2009.—Under sub-section (2) of
Section 32 of the Indian Veterinary Council Act, 1984 (Central
Act 52 of 1984), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby notifies
the following names of four members elected among
themselves by Veterinary Practitioners registered in the State
Veterinary Registers as members to the Tamil Nadu Veterinary
Council under clause (a) of sub-Section (1) of Section 32
of the said Act:—

COMMERCIAL TAXES AND REGISTRATION
DEPARTMENT
Remission of Stamp Duty chargeable for instrument of
Agreement for Finance executed by the Self Help
Groups, Panchayat Level Federations and Economic
Activity Federations under Indian Stamp Act.
[G.O. Ms. No. 158,  Commercial Taxes and Registration
(J1), 5th November 2009, Aippasi 19, Thiruvalluvar
Aandu 2040.]
No. II(2)/CTR/610/2009.—In exercise of the powers
conferred by clause (a) of sub-section (1) of Section 9 of
the Indian Stamp Act, 1899 (Central Act II of 1899), the
Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby remits the duty chargeable
under the said Act in respect of instruments of Agreement
for Finance, Inter-se-Agreement among members, Deed of
Hypothecation and Deed of Mortgage executed by the
Self Help Groups, Federation of Self Help Groups at Panchayat
level i.e., Panchayat Level Federations and Economic Activity
Federations, promoted by the Rural Development and
Panchayat Raj Department in favour of Banks, for
obtaining loan.
RAJEEV RANJAN,
Principal Secretary to Government.
ENVIRONMENT AND FORESTS DEPARTMENT
Notifications under Tamil Nadu Forest Act
Declaration of Megamalai Forest Block in Andipatty
Taluk of Theni District as Reserved Forests
under the Act.
[G.O. Ms. No. 118, Environment and Forest (FR-14),
9th September 2009.]
No. II(2)/EF/611/2009.—In exercise of the powers conferred
by Section 16 of the Tamil Nadu Forest Act, 1882
(Tamil Nadu Act V of 1882), the Governor of Tamil Nadu
hereby declares the area, boundaries of which are specified
in the schedule below, as reserved forest with effect on and
from 31-5-2010:—

BOUNDARIES.
North.--Starting from the junction point of Survey Field
Number 44, 45 and 80 of Village Number 21 Kadamalaikundu
and Survey Field Number 280 (Part) of Village number 23
Megamalai village, the boundary generally runs East, South
East and South along the Southern side of Survey Field
number 80, Western side of Survey Field numbers 81, 82,
83 and 90, Northern, Western side of Survey Field number
92, Western side of Survey Field numbers 93, 94, 95, 116,
117, 118, 119 and 120 till it reaches the South West corner
of Survey Field number 120 thence the boundary generally
runs West and South East along the Northern side of survey
field Number 134, Northern and Western side of Survey Field
number 135, Western side of Survey Field number 136,
Northern and Western side of Survey Field number 140,

417.38.0
Declaration of Oothukadu Forest Block in Valangaiman
Taluk of Thiruvarur District as Reserved Forest under
the Act.
[G.O. Ms. No. 125, Environment and Forests (FR 14),
22nd September 2009.]
No. II(2)/EF/612/2009.—In exercise of the powers conferred
by Section 16 of the Tamil Nadu Forest Act, 1882 (Tamil
Nadu Act V of 1882), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby
declares the area, the boundaries of which are specified in
the Schedule below as Reserved Forest with effect on and
from 31st May 2010:
THE SCHEDULE
1. Name of District
:
Thiruvarur
2. Name of The Taluk
:
Valangaiman
3. Number and name of
:
8. Oothukadu
the Village
4. Survey Field Number
:
508/1A
5. Name of the Forest Block
:
Oothukadu Forest Block
6. Extent of the Forest Block
:
0.99.0 hectare.
BOUNDARIES
North.— Starting from the junction point of Survey Field
Numbers 522/A, 522/B, 508/1A and 568 of Village No. 8,
Oothukadu Village, the boundary runs towards east along the
southern side Survery Field Number 568 and reaches
the trijunction point of Survey Field Numbers 508/1B, 568
and 508/1A.
East.— Thence it runs towards south along the western
side of Survey Field Number 508/1B and reaches the trijunction
point of Survey Field Numbers 508/1B, 522/B and 508/1A.
South and West.— Thence it runs towards west along
the northern side of Survey Field Number 522/B and reaches
the starting point.
ADMITTED RIGHTS
Nil
DEBENDRANATH SARANGI,
Principal Secretary to Government.
HIGHWAYS AND MINOR PORTS DEPARTMENT
Acquisition of Lands
[G.O. Ms. No. 219, Highways and Minor Ports (HW2),
11th November 2009, Aippasi 26, Thiruvalluvar
Aandu-2040.]
No. II(2)/HWMP/613/2009.—The Government of Tamil
Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the
schedule below are required for formation of link Road and
Reconstruction of High Level Bridge across Palar river and it
having already been decided that the entire amount of
compensation to be awarded for the lands is to be paid out
of the funds controlled and managed by the Divisional Engineer
NABARD and Rural Roads Division, Chengalpattu and after
having considered the cause shown by the owner or other

person having interest in the said lands, as the case may be,
hereby publish the following Notice under the sub-section (1)
of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001
(Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002).
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu
Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002), the Governor
of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the land specified in the
Schedule below measuring 0.38.5 hectare to the same, a
little more or less, required for the formation of link Road
and Reconstruction of High Level Bridge across Palar River.
The plan of the land is kept in the office of the Divisional
Engineer (H) NABARD and Rural Roads Division, Chengalpattu
may be inspected at any time during office hours.
THE SCHEDULE
Kancheepuram District, Uthiramerur Taluk,
88, Thirumukkudal Village.
Government, Ryotwari, Punjai S.No. 45/3A, Now sub-
Divided as 45/3A2, belonging to registered holder Sri Appan
Venkatesa Perumal Koil, bounded on the north by S.No. 284,
east and south by S.No. 45/4 and west by S.No. 45/3A—
0.36.5. hectare.
Government, Ryotwari, Punjai S.No. 60, Now sub-divided
as 60/1, belonging to Registered holder Thiru V. Gopal Pillai,
son of A. Veeraraghava Pillai, bounded on the north by
S.No. 45/3B, east by S.No. 60, south by S.No. 62/1 and west
by S.No. 45/3C—0.02.0 hectare.
Total—0.38.5 hectare.
G. SANTHANAM,
Secretary to Government.
HOME DEPARTMENT
Grant of licence to grant certificates of marriage between
Indian Christians under Indian Christian Marriage
Act.
[G.O.Ms.No. 844, Home (Cts.IV), 30th September 2009.]
No. II(2)/HO/614/2009.—The Governor of Tamil Nadu,
under and by virtue of the authority contained in and Conferred
by Section 9 of the Indian Christian Marriage Act, 1872 (Central
Act XV of 1872), hereby grants a license to Thiru M. George
Baktha Singh, No. 7, Thulukanathamman Koil Street,
Pallikarani, Tambaram, Kancheepuram District. To grant
Certificates of marriage between Indian Christians in
accordance the said Act, within the territories comprising the
State of Tamil Nadu.
D. JOTHI JAGARAJAN,
Secretary to Government.
(In-charge)
HOUSING AND URBAN DEVELOPMENT
DEPARTMENT.
Exemption from certain Provisions of the Development
Regulations of the Second Master Plan for Chennai
Metropolitan Area relating to Reservation of land for
communal and recreational purposes under Tamil Nadu
Town and Country Planning Act.
[G.O.Ms.No. 196, Housing and Urban Development (UD I),
10th November 2009.]
No. II(2)/HOU/615/2009.—In exercise of powers conferred
by Section 113 of the Tamil Nadu Town and country Planning
Act, 1971 (Tamil Nadu Act 35 of 1972), the Governor of Tamil
Nadu hereby exempts the land in T.S. No. 2/D and
2/F, Block No. 6 of Kanagam Village, Rajiv Gandhi Road
(OMR), Taramani, Chennai from the item 1(c) of Annexure
XX, referred to in sub-regulation (8) of Regulation 28 of
Development Regulations of Second Master Plan for Chennai
Metropolitan Area 2026 relating to Reservation of land for
communal and recreational purposes, for the proposed
construction of DBF + GF + 11 Floors +12th Floor part
building for IIT Madras Research Park (with shops,
Restaurants, Offices, Food Court, Incubations, Auditoriums,
80 Guest Rooms and Canteens) by the Registrar, IIT Madras
Subject to the condition that the applicant shall maintain the
open Space Reservation area earmarked only as park and
play field and not for any other purpose and that any violation
in this regard shall be dealt with by the Chennai Metropolitan
Development Authority Appropriately.
SURJIT K CHAUDHARY,
Principal Secretary to Government.
LABOUR AND EMPLOYMENT DEPARTMENT
Disputes between Workmen and Managements referred
to Labour Courts for adjudication.

Üó² ¶¬í„ ªêòô£÷˜.
MUNICIPAL ADMINISTRATION AND WATER SUPPLY
DEPARTMENT.
List of Parks, in the areas within the Jurisdiction of the
Thiruthurai poondi Municipality under the Tamil Nadu
Parks, Play-fields and Open Spaces (Preservation and
Regulation) Act.
[G.O. Ms. No. 215, Municipal Administration and
Water Supply (MA5), 11th November 2009.]
No.II(2)/MAWS/625/2009.—In exercise of the powers
conferred by sub-section (2) of Section 3 of the Tamil Nadu
Parks, Play-fields and Open Spaces (Preservation and
Regulation) Act, 1959 (Tamil Nadu Act 26 of 1959), the
Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby publishes the list of parks in
the areas specified in the Schedule below within the jurisdiction
of the Thiruthuraipoondi Municipality.
2. The maps, plans and documents relating to the said
park will be available to the public for inspection at the
Municipal Office, Thiruthuraipoondi between 10.00 a.m. and
5.45 p.m. on all working days.
3. Any person interested, may submit his objections or
suggestions, if any, in writing in respect of anything contained
in, or relating to, the list aforesaid, to the Government within
three months from the date of the publication of this Notification
in the Thiruvarur District Gazette.
4. Objections or suggestions, if any, should be addressed
to the Secretary to Government, Municipal Administration and
Water Supply Department, Secretariat, Chennai-600 009.
